mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B5%B7%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%A2%81%E8%80%80%E6%95%8F%E7%AD%89%E5%9B%9B%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-440738.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁展鸿</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东深圳市福田区法轮功学员，女士，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，梁展鸿老人在家中被抓捕，所谓的原因是她给小区保安讲法轮功被举报。遭受绑架几个月后，梁展鸿老人从福田看守所转入南山看守所，目前已经被非法关押在南山看守所将近一年。后得知已遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，未上诉。目前已收到通知，将被送广州女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁子亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人，梁子亮与妻子李银秀，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廖光慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川绵阳市涪城区新华厂家属区法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日下午，廖光慧，被十几个身穿便衣的彪形大汉（后了解是花园派出所警察）突然闯入家中，未出示任何搜捕证和身份证明等，就强行控制家人自由行动，像土匪一样抄家近三个小时之久，强行抢走私人物品：笔记本计算机</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">台，手机、打印机、刻录机、现金几百元，大法书籍、大法师父法像等个人物品。廖光慧被关押在绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日被绵阳市涪城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金三千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廖杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、大连市庄河市法轮功学员。廖杰于<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日出生，家居庄河市长岭镇。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，她在蓉花山镇双烈寺集讲真相被蓉花山镇派出所警察抓捕。当日下午，警察上门抄家，抢劫了一些私人物品。廖杰被关押在姚家看守所，后被构陷到庄河市法院，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廖小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省梅州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，她开始修炼法轮功。因持续宣传法轮功，曾遭劳教、拘留。因发真相资料被监控查到，廖小平<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午被当地五洲派出所抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被梅州市梅县区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，罚款一万五千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/25/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E6%A2%85%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%BB%96%E5%B0%8F%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440476.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/25/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E6%A2%85%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%BB%96%E5%B0%8F%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440476.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林春芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，湖北省丹江口市人，原丹江口市丁家营镇丁营大道<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号村民、丹江口市南水北调中线工程库区农村移民，现北京市海淀区黄庄小区<span lang="EN-US">813</span>楼<span lang="EN-US">312</span>室居民，基督徒，维权访民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。早年，曾因是湖北省丹江口市南水北调中线工程库区的农村移民，理应得到的政府占地补偿款一直未能得到，随向村镇等各级管理部门“反映问题”，自此屡遭打压；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因自家房屋面临强拆，其及与其同住的父母在拒强拆中遭殴打，情急之下 ，其用汽油欲自焚以示抗议；事后其虽赶到当地警局报案，但竟了无结果，当局依然不予公正、恰当解决；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因上访而被丹江口市丁家营镇警方刑拘，并被关进丹江口市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，又被丹江口市警方以“扰乱单位秩序”、“阻碍执行职务”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，再被当地警方关进黑监狱，且其房屋被夷为平地，屋内贵重物品均丢失，财产、财务及家畜等尽遭掩埋和损坏；后其因此继续上访，并到北京寻求信访帮助，不料遭到更多的侮辱欺凌、拘押和关黑监狱等迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因住京维权遭截访，先被关在丹江口市驻京办招待所，后又被秘押至丹江口市文华宾馆<span lang="EN-US">103</span>房间，并被强行脱光衣服搜身，致其倍感羞辱，曾为此绝食抗议<span lang="EN-US">7</span>昼夜；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，又被更换地址持续秘关<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，期间遭十几名看守其的黑社会性质的男性青年多次殴打和虐待，致其因痛不欲生，拔下窗户上的钉子割腕自杀；后幸免遇难，但仍被当局强逼写材料，不写就打；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其被迫在丁家营镇政府提供的协议书上签字画押，并写下不再上访保证书，才终得获释返家；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因在京上访期间，受到北京基督教圣爱团契家庭教会对其生活及信仰上的帮助与支持，随与教会信徒们一起学习《圣经》，并于次年受洗而成为一名基督徒；之后，其信访要求有所解决，地方政府为其及父母修盖了房子，作为其在水库移民中的经济补偿（当然还有土地等其他问题并未解决），而其此时也在北京结婚，其丈夫因是北京公民并在北京工作当医生，随其成为名副其实的北京媳妇，并与丈夫长居京城。之后，因其原籍住宅的户主名字，在当年登记的是其父母之名而非其本人，随其在父母明确授意的前提下，多次向有关部门提出申请，要求将户主姓名更为自己的姓名，然而相关政府部门却对其申请久拖未予解决，其随被迫再次在京信访投诉；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被丹江口市警方以“寻衅滋事”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被原籍截访人员突然带走，遣回原籍后被丹江口市十堰市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，并被关押在十堰市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被丹江口市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，追溯其曾于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来一直因房屋拆迁问题在国家非信访部门上访，此行为已与现行相关法律规条相抵触，又加之中共十•一<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年党庆将至，为防止其再度维权上访，给党庆造成不良影响，故而被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被湖北省丹江口市法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。目前在湖北省武汉女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">(</span>湖北省武汉市乔口区宝丰一路<span lang="EN-US">97</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">430030)</span>服刑。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/4_19.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/4_19.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林海英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。李瑞华林海英母女<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在家中被官渡公安警察分别处以形式拘留和取保候审。据<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华区检察院的指控，李瑞华<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许，在昆明市官渡区人民东路向过往群众散发 “为你而来”光盘并宣扬法轮功时被昆明市公安局官渡分局金马派出所协警抓捕、抢劫法轮功光盘<span lang="EN-US">5</span>片，公安警察赶到现场后将抓捕，后搜查李瑞华和林海英共同居住的房间，当场抓捕了林海英，同时抢劫了大量法轮功真相资料及光盘，不法警察搜查过程中，林海英多次制止警察犯法，朝窗户向小区高呼“法轮大法好”等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，李瑞华和林海英母女被五华法院开庭；林海英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千，李瑞华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至：林海英<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林乐宏：女，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，大学本科毕业，家住深圳市南山区。林乐宏和马彦平都暂在深圳龙岗区布吉镇大芬油画村租住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上，林乐宏、马彦平在大芬油画村租住房内，被龙岗区公安分局国保及布吉派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家，两人被关押到龙岗区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，警察再次对<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人的租住房进行了查抄，将法轮功书籍、资料、电脑、打印机、塑封机、切边机、硬盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等个人物品全部劫走。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，林乐宏、马彦平被龙岗区检察院批捕。被关押后，林乐宏多次绝食反迫害，遭看守所强制灌食，健康受到严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，林乐宏被强制灌食后，被送医院所谓“抢救”。从此，林乐宏吃什么吐什么，回到看守所后，身体<span lang="EN-US">1</span>直不好。血压高至<span lang="EN-US">160/180mmHg</span>（低血压高）。她每周需要吸氧<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次，只能吃流食，出现心口痛，左手麻木。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，林乐宏、马彦平被盐田区法院庭审。有律师出庭做无罪辩护。为了抵制持续的迫害，从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日始，林乐宏又开始绝食，被连续强制灌食<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多天。体重只剩<span lang="EN-US">46</span>公斤，舌根发硬，吞咽困难，胸口时常发闷，血糖极低（不到<span lang="EN-US">3mmol/L</span>），手脚冰凉，特别怕冷，<span lang="EN-US">26</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">︒</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">的气温下还要穿大棉袄。在林乐宏身体健康严重受损的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，盐田区法院宣判，林乐宏被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；马彦平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/28/%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E6%9E%97%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%8F%E3%80%81%E9%A9%AC%E5%BD%A6%E5%B9%B3%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-440593.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/28/%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E6%9E%97%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%8F%E3%80%81%E9%A9%AC%E5%BD%A6%E5%B9%B3%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-440593.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林丽卿：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月十<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，林丽卿到揭阳市榕城区法轮功学员林玩贞家读《转法轮》，被前来骚扰的榕城区国保大队伙同揭阳市榕华派出所警察抓捕。当时，在林玩贞家读《转法轮》的还有法轮功学员吴荣端。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨，林玩贞、吴荣端被释放。林丽卿则一直被关押于揭阳市看守所。林玩贞由于被惊吓过度，被释放一个多月后去世。后得知她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林丽珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日茂名市茂南区法院主审法官柯学军宣判：林丽珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万；林燕梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金八千；吴朝棋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林茂成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连市金州区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，林茂成给陌生人讲法轮功，被他诬告后遭抓捕抄家，非法拿走大法书籍、计算机、打印机、身份证、驾驶证等物品。林茂成被劫持到派出所期间强制照相，录指纹、声音、验血、做完笔录后，逼他签字未果。半夜后，人被放回，监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，林茂成被大连普兰店检察院批捕，并被大连大孤山边防派出所强制关押在大连开发区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，林茂成被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：辽宁省沈阳市著名维权人士林明洁的哥哥。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与弟弟林明洁一起遭抓捕，后被被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见林明洁是才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">是辽宁省沈阳市铁西区人，原辽宁省某国企技术人员，人称“访民义侠”，维权公民，人权捍卫者，曾获得海外中国民主党颁发的曹顺利勇气奖。早年因不服其兄林明华被行政拘留和家里拆迁补偿的问题而走上信访之路，后因长期到京上访，并热心为访民维权发声而屡遭当局非法绑架、关押、拘留等打击迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁因在北京国家信访局、住建部反映地方政府违法强拆事宜，被沈阳市驻京办等截访人员跟踪骚扰，后被强行遣返原籍，并被沈阳市铁西区警方予以刑事拘留，一个月后才得以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又因和一批沈阳访民在中国公安部六部口信访局集体上访（简称“集访”），状告沈阳市公安局与局长许文有徇私枉法，随后被沈阳市截访人员抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被沈阳市铁西区警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并控诉其罪状：在北京多次集访扰乱公共秩序、在庆安徐纯合案时打出“我是访民，朝我开枪”的标语、长期将访民维权的新闻发给境外媒体等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日止。此前曾被羁押于沈阳市铁西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，林明洁结束两年多的监狱生活刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与哥哥林明华一起遭警方抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林炎德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九六五年四月出生，家住揭阳市空港区渔湖镇港口村。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，林炎德在使用真相基站发送信息时，被揭阳市公安局空港分局国保和渔湖派出所警察蹲守抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，法院到揭阳市看守所宣判，林炎德被判重刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，他被关押到广东省四会监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林燕梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日茂名市茂南区法院主审法官柯学军宣判：林丽珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万；林燕梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金八千；吴朝棋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林在务：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，化名林大海、林忠，福建省福清市人，福清市东瀚镇东瀚村田尾<span lang="EN-US">17</span>号村民，职业不详，“耶和华见证人”信徒、传道人，新疆耶和华见证人教会正规先驱（类似于基督教的长老），中国在押良心犯。因信仰耶和华见证人教派，并被委任在新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒地区做正规先驱（即该教会一种重要职务），在库尔勒市组成家庭聚会，举行上百次大型聚会及成员培训，大力发展信徒，随遭极左思维极强的中共当局严打狠批；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在“耶和华见证人案”大抓捕中，被库尔勒市警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”与多人悉数抓捕、刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式逮捕，并被指控称，其因打着基督教旗号，组织教会聚会， “宣扬所谓政治中立，煽动成员及他人不履行公民法定义务”，破坏了国家的法律法规，所以属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人涉邪教案被警方向当地检察院提起公诉；后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被检察院发回补侦，但同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又已被补查重报；至今待审未判，且无更多具体信息；据悉，曾在看守所内因拒绝唱“红歌”等，常遭连体铐、抱铐等体罚虐待。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘爱华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省辽阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，辽阳市警察跟踪刘爱华。刘爱华被抓捕、抄家，关押在辽阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，刘爱华被灯塔市检察院批捕，后被起诉到灯塔市法院。刘爱华被关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">202</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被灯塔市法院第一次庭审，当日未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点，刘爱华被灯塔市法院第二次开庭后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/2/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432066.html#21101225216-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘伯滨</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：哈尔滨市香坊区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年毕业于湖南大学，原为哈尔滨量具刃具厂（国有企业）高级工程师，由于坚持修炼使她受益的法轮大法，曾经被判刑五年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>至<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市、区三十多名法轮功学员被绑架，刘伯滨<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被香坊区警察抓捕、抄家、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日上午刘伯滨被哈尔滨市道里区法院视频远程开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、罚金二万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘长富</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘长富并抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对刘长富、李国爱、吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。刘长富刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘春静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，因修炼法轮功，刘春静<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年曾被劳教两年，送佳木斯市西格木劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘春静在发放真相传单时，被人恶意构陷，又遭恶警抓捕被桦南县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，关押到黑龙江女子监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在街上递送给人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个护身符卡片，被举报，桦南县胜利派出所警察将刘春静抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘春静<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘春琴</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：湖南省株洲市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，原湖南省衡阳轧钢厂职工，一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，刘春琴多次被绑架、非法关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被株洲市天元区公安分局泰山路派出所恶警绑架；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被株洲市芦淞区法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被送湖南省女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘翠梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘达鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林榆树市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。原籍吉林省舒兰市人，后搬到榆树市，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮功。因信仰法轮功曾被劳教和判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刘达鹏与妻子李春环因在楼下自家车的车筐里发现别人放的真相资料，然后顺便发出去，被人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，榆树市正阳派出所五个警察闯入刘达鹏、李春环夫妇家中，将二人抓捕。刘达鹏被刑事拘留，妻子李春环被拘留五天。由于疫情，刘达鹏被取保候审一年，他们没被关在拘留所，而是被关押在正阳派出所，两天后，刘达鹏与妻子李春环被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，正阳派出所打电话让刘达鹏和李春环到派出所去一趟，刘达鹏被构陷到德惠市检察院，被批捕，并关押在榆树市看守所。后刘达鹏被德惠法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘德明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏南通维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日一早，无执法权的南通欣宏房屋征收服务有限公司受南通市港闸区住房和建设环境保护局委托，雇佣一批保安拥着挖掘机（犯罪工具），进入南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村，将刘德明的房屋团团围住，并拉上了警戒线，企图强拆，以达到非法圈地的目的。村民们向<span lang="EN-US">110</span>报警。港闸公安分局民警到达现场后，只是谈谈地说了一句：“政府行为，我们管不了”，致使非法圈地的保安更加有恃无恐，对刘德明家围困了整整一夜。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，该公司雇佣的保安用铁锤敲打刘德明的房屋。情势危急，且在民警不作为的情况下，刘德明为捍卫家园才点燃钩机。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，南通市公安局港闸分局以涉嫌故意毁坏财产罪为由，将南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村村民刘德明带走调查。次日，该局作出港公（公）拘通字【<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>】<span lang="EN-US">263</span>号拘留通知书，载明对刘德明刑事拘留，现羁押于南通市看守所，并将拘留通知书向刘德明妻子送达。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘富祥</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：重庆维权人士。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刘富祥刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘广：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。男，职业医生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，警察闯入刘广有家诊所，将法轮功书籍掠走，并将刘广有抓捕关押、刑拘。后移交佳木斯市向阳区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日分别被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘广有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘国花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省大理州宾川县法轮功学员。一九六八年出生，家住大理州宾川县金牛镇太和农场柳家湾十五队。刘国花曾因向世人赠送神韵晚会光碟遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刘国花于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被抓捕，之后一直被关押在大理州看守所。在家属完全不知情的情况下，就对刘国花开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/15/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E5%88%98%E5%9B%BD%E8%8A%B1%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440088.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘海康：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江北安市法轮功学员。刘海康于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在家被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘海康的家人才得知刘海康已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现仍被关押在北安市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘汗：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"> </span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士刘富祥的儿子。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刘汗刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘洪兰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘洪兰、赵根法、黄春玲、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。刘洪兰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘红枢</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：又名刘红书，陕西省岐山县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，岐山县京当镇祝家庄社区西戢村营西组人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，刘红枢修炼法轮大法。在法轮大法遭受迫害的最初那几年，刘红枢在新疆打工，在一家出版社工作，在讲法轮功被当地“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”人员绑架、失去了正常工作的机会，被非法劳教。此后经常受到岐山县、祝家庄乡政府人员的骚扰、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在家里被岐山县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>人员抓捕抄家，关押在岐山县看守所，后来被秘密开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘会茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，河北省人，知名民营企业家、河北大午农牧集团有限公司前董事长孙大午之妻，河北大午农牧有限公司核心创办人（之一），企业前高层管理者，挂职副监事长，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年起，因承包了一片荒弃的砖窑和坟包地作为投资养殖业，后历经几年发展，随促成与其丈夫孙大午共同创建河北大午农牧集团有限公司之行为，并成为丈夫创业、经营发展以及日后对社会“行公义，好怜悯”等作为的坚实后盾；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，因河北大午农牧集团有限公司孙大午等<span lang="EN-US">25</span>位集团高管及亲属、亲信幕僚等被河北省高碑店市警方悉数带走，并被迅速以涉嫌“寻衅滋事、破坏生产经营罪”指定居所监视居住，其受牵连亦与两个儿媳等分别被带走、刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其年事已高，又患高血压、糖尿病等多种疾病，且早已不参与大午集团的决策和经营，既不涉及违法犯罪，也不涉及暴力性犯罪，其代理律师随为其先后两次申请变更强制措施（即取保候审），但两次均被警方以“经审查，我局认为刘会茹有可能毁灭、伪造证据、干扰证人作证“为由遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被高碑店市警方以涉嫌“非法吸收公众存款罪”转正式逮捕；后其案被高碑店市检察院起诉至至高碑店市法院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，终被河北省高碑店市法院一审以“非法吸收公众存款罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同案另两个儿媳及一个侄女被判定罪免罚。目前被羁押于河北省保定市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘家玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津静海县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年四十六岁。原静海县市容环卫局干部，静海县静海镇高庄子村人。她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年两次被非法关押在天津大港区板桥女子劳教所，前后五年遭受强制奴役劳动、不让睡觉等迫害，她坚持信仰，不妥协。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年才出狱。刘家玲<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，被关押在天津女子监狱，遭受残忍迫害。刘家玲在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又失踪，后得知被关押在静海看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获知刘家玲又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘建民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北邯郸市魏县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刘建民在广东省珠海市打工，在外面写“法轮大法好”标语，还百姓知情权。随后刘建民被珠海市斗门区国保大队抓捕到当地派出所拘留，后被批捕，并被起诉到珠海市斗门区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，刘建民被珠海市斗门区法院庭审，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前被非法关押在珠海市斗门区第二看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘建霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省三门峡人，五十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七二零后，因去北京为法轮大法鸣冤而遭抓捕，后被非法劳教，劫持到郑州十八里河劳教所，后来又被三门峡法院判刑六年。她曾被迫流离失所多年。三门峡“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>” 到处查找她，在全国非法通缉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刘建霞与法轮功学员杨中省被跟踪抓捕。刘建霞曾在河南省新乡女子监狱被关小号折磨<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多天，被迫害得脸肿、胸闷等“哮喘”症状已经一年多，现在越来越重，生命垂危，据悉每天靠大量药物维持生存。当年与刘建霞一起被抓捕的法轮功学员杨中省，被非法关押没有几天，就于二零一六年四月在郑州第三看守所被迫害致死。刘建霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">福建福州维权人士。福州市仓山区城门镇前锦村村民。刘建新因房屋被强拆近<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，至今无补偿、无安置<span lang="EN-US">.</span>在去年，刘建新因在家被<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时监控，感到非常郁闷，去北京旅游散心，结果遭到维稳人员劫持后被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。因为刘建新在北京既没有信访，更没有违法行为，最后公安只能将其放了。后来，当时的城门镇赵书记就刘建新的诉求组织了一次协调，因为政府不愿意就其违法强拆行为，依法给予安置与赔偿，双方协商未能成功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刘建新在北京永定门河边举“冤”字牌，然后跳下去准备了此被官府肆意欺压与压迫的屈辱一生，然后被保安救上来。到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>号晩上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点左右，刘建新被送到城门派岀所，关在城门派岀所铁笼里面，其妻子得知消息后赶到，一直等到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号晚上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点之后，派出所告知刘建新被送走了。后获悉其被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被正式批捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘建新从福州市看守所给妻子江国英寄出书信，称当局已对构陷他的所谓寻衅滋事罪一案，在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日进行秘密开庭，公诉机关建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年！其妻子证实，一审仓山区法院没有通知家属旁听。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_85.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_85.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_6.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_6.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘杰（黑龙江）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江哈尔滨市宾县维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的刘杰，是因为在<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年做生意时，经销的<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余万商品被检察院扣押拒不返回、且销毁案件的案卷材料而上访。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，刘杰在北京时，哈尔滨市宾县政府的领导多次给刘杰打电话，说别去国家信访局登记了，回来就给解决问题，还给刘杰买了机票回宾县。当刘杰回宾县后，政法委书记刘宇峰确实组织了听证会，但提出给予<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万困难补助，一次性解决刘杰的诉求，刘杰拒绝了这样的解决方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘杰因对由政法委书记刘宇峰组织的听证结果表达不满，被宾县公安局以辱骂了政法委书记刘宇峰为由拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年“七一”建党百年前夕，宾县公安局曾以刘杰在今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日到检察院辱骂工作人员为由，又以“寻衅滋事”为由对刘杰拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天。今年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘杰再次去北京上访，在北京拦截了国家信访局大局长李文章的车，被宾县公安局以“寻衅滋事”为由拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。后刘杰的女儿接到辖区派出所电话，告知其父亲已经被刑事拘留，送看守所羁押。刘杰的女儿问自己父亲已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周岁了，之前已两次被行政拘留，是否符合合并为刑事拘留的规定？派出所没有给予回答。据了解，刘杰患有严重高血压、高血压脂、心脏病，且是<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周岁的老人了，已不符合羁押式拘留的规定，现在宾县公安又升级为刑事拘留，看来一心想要维护合法权益的刘老汉是凶多吉少了。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，刘又杰被被举报单位宾县检察院正式批捕。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/70.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/70.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘金焕</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：广州市番禺区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，毕业于广东省建材中专，原番禺水泥厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚上，刘金焕往停在钟村优瑞厂附近的小车门把手上放了几份有关疫情的周报，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，番禺区公安分局国保与钟村派出所出动<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台警车，对刘金焕抓捕抄家，并将刘金焕关押到番禺区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘金萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员。刘金萍于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被警察抓捕、抄家。当地公安、检察院以涉嫌所谓“破坏法律实施”的罪名将她刑事拘留，并将构陷材料递交到向阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">311</span>日佳木斯市向阳区法院对此开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日向阳区法院对刘金萍判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。收到判决书后，刘金萍委托亲友辩护人上诉。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，佳木斯市中院违反法律程序，剥夺亲友辩护人的权利，没有公开开庭审理就做出了驳回上诉、维持原判的终审裁定。目前刘金萍被关押在佳木斯市看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/13/%E4%BD%B3%E6%9C%A8%E6%96%AF%E5%88%98%E9%87%91%E8%90%8D%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%8A%E8%AF%89-%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%A4-441238.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁沈阳的维权人士。刘丽是为父亲刘树义劳工权益而上访了十一年。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，时年已经<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的刘树义为了活命，还在沈阳市苏家屯八一镇政府内烧锅炉，为里面“全心全意为人民服务”的官员做苦力。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">19</span>点，加班的刘树义在上班途中遭遇车祸，按照劳动合同法的规定，用人单位应该以工伤予以补偿，但八一镇政府因为没有为劳动者办理工伤保险，就拒绝承担工伤责任，作为女儿的刘丽开始替父上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘丽到了北京府右街后被截访送马家楼，然而有沈阳市苏家屯区的截访人员接回。后遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刘丽因“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被检察院批捕。暂无案件后续信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘丽杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span><span lang="EN-US"> </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生于黑龙江省佳木斯市，毕业于东北师范大学生物系，在佳木斯市职教集团职业学院学报编辑部任职（该职业学院的前身是佳木斯市教育学院）。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年她开始修炼法轮功，连年被学院评为优秀教师。刘丽杰于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被当地国保警察抓捕，后以“取保候审”回家。之后，刘丽杰仍被当局构陷到向阳区检察院，法院对她实施期限半年的“监视居住”，在她家的楼旁安了监控摄像头，有便衣警察带车蹲守。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日早上，刘丽杰和家人到派出所索要所谓的“监视居住”通知书时，被带到了法院。法院刑庭庭长宋涛问刘丽杰是否认罪认罚，刘丽杰拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，建设派出所所长和向阳公安分局国保大队长门茂盛来到刘丽杰家，说她写“<span lang="EN-US">3</span>书”（放弃修炼的所谓“保证书”等）的话，检察院和法院的人说了，她的事就会缓下来。刘丽杰仍然拒绝。后遭关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日<span lang="EN-US"> ,</span>在没有辩护人出庭、被告人的辩护权没有获得保障的情况下，刘丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.ntdtv.com/gb/2021/12/01/a103282257.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.ntdtv.com/gb/2021/12/01/a103282257.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘明萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省宁波市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘明萍被宁波江北区庄桥派出所警察抓捕抄家。后获悉刘明萍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被关押到浙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘平</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：大午集团集团总经理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。刘平被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、非法占用农用地罪、寻衅滋事罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：刘被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">95</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘鹏华： </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">佳士案维权工人。“<span lang="EN-US">7.27</span>大抓捕”第<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初，刘鹏华、余浚聪、米久平、李展等四人被正式逮捕。案件接近两年，仍无音信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘强<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，刘强等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括刘强在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。刘强被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省聊城市开发区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，聊城市东阿县顾官屯乡扒棍刘村人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，刘庆良曾被中共劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日刘庆良被德州市齐河县公安局国保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被齐河县法院用视频方式开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省铁岭市清河区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，多次被迫害，被非法拘留、非法劳教、两次被非法判刑（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年），累计非法刑期达<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年之多。她遭吊铐、电击、冻等惨无人道的折磨，曾经在马三家劳教所被摧残精神失常。刘庆香<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在市场讲真相时，被清河区公安分局国保大抓捕、并抄家。刘庆香被关押在铁岭市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份被清河区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆余：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市大石桥市法轮功学员刘庆余，，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十日，中共江泽民团伙开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，刘庆余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被中共人员抓捕、劳教、判刑，曾在公安局、看守所、劳教所遭受酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，刘庆余被不明真相的人恶意举报，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刘庆余和妻子张畅被抓捕。刘庆余遭刑讯逼供，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被关押在大石桥看守所。妻子张畅被关押到营口市看守所，第<span lang="EN-US">38</span>天被释放。营口市站前区法院通知律师于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午在大石桥市看守所庭审。刘庆余被营口市站前区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/24/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%88%98%E5%BA%86%E4%BD%99%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-433960.html"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘仁秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市旅顺法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前被关押在大连市监狱第五监区。据悉，监狱非法剥夺了他家人的探视权。家人已经有约半年多的时间没有见到他了。刘仁秋是在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被特警在其租住房内抓捕。当天，大连政法委策划，采用手机监控、跟踪、定位、蹲坑等手段，在大连地区各县区同一时间统一行动，抓捕了数十名法轮功学员，有很多人当天被放回，有的当月回家，最后还有多人被判刑。这次抓捕被公安国保称为“<span lang="EN-US">1614</span>”大案。刘仁秋、盛杰、谷树春、王红玉四名法轮功学员，被旅顺法院二次非法开完庭后，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下判决书， 刘仁秋被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚款五万元；盛杰<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半、罚款三万元；王红玉<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚金款三千。刘仁秋刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘汝兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东青岛胶州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，山东省青岛胶州市洋河镇人。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，刘汝兰在打工处，又被胶州市公安局中云派出所警察抓捕，后被关押到青岛市即墨普东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日下午被青岛市黄岛区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘瑞莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。家住河北丰宁满族自治县大阁镇南岗子村，丰宁满族自治县残疾妇女，法轮功学员。在中共对法轮功<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年的迫害中，刘瑞莲曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、劳教两次：<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年（提前释放）；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年再次被劳教（勒索<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元，劳教两年）。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚在家里被抓捕，抢走复印机、电脑、电视、<span lang="EN-US">VCD</span>等。关押<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。这一次是<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日在家中被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被开庭，律师做无罪辩护，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日得到消息，刘瑞莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，随后刘瑞莲上诉，结果被维持原判，于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日送石家庄女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">14</span>监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘若寒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市河北区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，刘若寒被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，天津市河北区法院二审开庭，维持一审原判，判处刘若寒<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刘若寒现已被送往天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘尚柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐山市玉田县法轮功学员。家住唐山市玉田县窝洛沽镇贾言庄村，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日早晨<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点左右，被唐山国安、玉田县公安局、窝洛沽镇派出所十多人联合抓捕，并抄家，很多私人财产被警察掠走。于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被庭审。后得知，刘尚柱被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E5%94%90%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%89%E7%94%B0%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%88%98%E5%B0%9A%E6%9F%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-434007.html"><span
